The precomputed table for unpacking color values. 

Converts quant value in 0-\/N range into unpacked value in 0-\/255 range, with BISE unscrambling applied.

Indexed by \mbox{[}quant\+\_\+mode -\/ 4\mbox{]}\mbox{[}data\+\_\+value\mbox{]}.

\index{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables@{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables}!astcenc\_quantization.cpp@{astcenc\_quantization.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables}{color\_uquant\_to\_scrambled\_pquant\_tables}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_a834f3531350f3a55d6271b4dc18a223d} 
const uint8\+\_\+t color\+\_\+uquant\+\_\+to\+\_\+scrambled\+\_\+pquant\+\_\+tables\mbox{[}17\mbox{]}\mbox{[}256\mbox{]}}



The precomputed table for packing quantized color values. 

Converts quant value in 0-\/255 range into packed quant value in 0-\/N range, with BISE scrambling applied.

Indexed by \mbox{[}quant\+\_\+mode -\/ 4\mbox{]}\mbox{[}data\+\_\+value\mbox{]}. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source}{astcenc\+\_\+quantization.\+cpp}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source_l00338}{338}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\index{quant\_mode\_table@{quant\_mode\_table}!astcenc\_quantization.cpp@{astcenc\_quantization.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{quant\_mode\_table}{quant\_mode\_table}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_a67050b7e3e5e5c4ff2021c8f266dd903} 
const int8\+\_\+t quant\+\_\+mode\+\_\+table\mbox{[}10\mbox{]}\mbox{[}128\mbox{]}}



The precomputed quant mode storage table. 

Indexing by \mbox{[}integer\+\_\+count/2\mbox{]}\mbox{[}bits\mbox{]} gives us the quantization level for a given integer count and number of compressed storage bits. Returns -\/1 for cases where the requested integer count cannot ever fit in the supplied storage size. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source}{astcenc\+\_\+quantization.\+cpp}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{astcenc__quantization_8cpp_source_l00802}{802}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.
